Correct responses are given when errors are made. \r\n\r\nThis program is designed for training in Electronics Technology, Electrical Technology, Automotive Technology, Medical Technology, Robotics, HVAC and other occupations that require voltmeter testing.\r\n\r\nCan you identify shorts and opens in electrical and electronic circuits using ohmmeter measurements? Can you determine the faulty electrical part in a circuit by making ohmmeter measurements and applying theory? This program can give you practical practice in developing measurement and troubleshooting skills. \r\n\r\nSome of these activities can challenge even experienced electronics technicians!
